# Chart 1b Detailed Result Analysis Report

## 1. Report Purpose

This report records the Defects4J Chart 1b benchmark run and analysis for the AR-QIEA true Pareto test-suite minimization pipeline. The analysis follows `SPEC-AR-QIEA.md` as the source of truth and uses the existing `REPORT_EVERY_CHANGES/2026-06-16.md` report style.

## G. Pareto Front Detail

The table below lists every feasible front point available in the benchmark JSON: `2631` points total. Full solution bit vectors and all raw per-seed records are stored in `artifacts/pareto/chart1b_full_19-06-2026.json`; the Markdown table keeps the objective and diagnostic values readable while preserving every front point row.

## H. ROP / Redundancy Analysis

| Algorithm | Mean ROP across front entries | Min ROP | Max ROP | Mean selected count | Min selected count | Max selected count |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| `ar_qiea` | 0.893684 | 0.864187 | 0.931613 | 1062.78 | 981 | 1130 |
| `mo_qiea` | 0.904325 | 0.875153 | 0.935340 | 1070.50 | 997 | 1143 |
| `nsga2` | 0.883295 | 0.839506 | 0.914363 | 945.19 | 880 | 998 |
| `random_front` | 0.926795 | 0.827567 | 0.953488 | 1174.76 | 430 | 1804 |

Lower ROP indicates less redundant overlap among selected tests. On Chart 1b, ROP should be interpreted as diagnostic only, because the objective vector optimizes MSR, CGCC, and ETR under the CR constraint, not ROP directly. The sparse matrix also means selected_count and ETR are strongly affected by the many zero-coverage tests.

## I. Statistical Analysis

| Comparison | Wilcoxon p-value | AR-QIEA HV wins/losses/ties by seed | Interpretation |
|---|---:|---:|---|
| `ar_qiea` vs `mo_qiea` | 0.000000 | 29/1/0 | AR-QIEA significantly greater at alpha=0.05 |
| `ar_qiea` vs `nsga2` | 0.992270 | 7/23/0 | AR-QIEA not significantly greater |
| `ar_qiea` vs `random_front` | 0.001611 | 22/8/0 | AR-QIEA significantly greater at alpha=0.05 |

P1 gate from the user request, `HV(ar_qiea) >= HV(mo_qiea)` and `HV(ar_qiea) >= HV(random_front)` with p < 0.05: `PASS`.
Broader paper-style claim against NSGA-II on this Chart 1b run: `FAIL` because NSGA-II has higher mean HV and `ar_qiea_vs_nsga2` is not significant in AR-QIEA's favor.

## J. Detailed Interpretation

- Best mean HV: `nsga2` with `0.696205`.
- Largest mean Pareto front: `random_front` with `24.300000` points.
- Best mean MSR: `random_front` with `1.000000`.
- Best mean CGCC: `ar_qiea` with `1.000000`.
- Best mean ETR: `nsga2` with `0.705314`.
- Fastest mean runtime: `random_front` with `8.1319` seconds per seed.
- AR-QIEA beats the MO-QIEA ablation and random_front by mean HV with statistically significant paired Wilcoxon results.
- NSGA-II has the highest mean HV on Chart 1b, so this dataset does not support the stronger claim that AR-QIEA beats NSGA-II.
- The result supports the risk-adaptive ablation claim on this dataset, but not the full paper claim against all baselines.
- Limitation: Chart 1b uses synthetic P1 risk data and has 1,947 zero-coverage tests over the selected requirements, so result quality and ETR trade-offs are strongly shaped by sparsity.

## L. Reproduction Commands

Run dataset validation smoke:

```powershell
cd "D:\FPT\Study\2026\sem5\SWT301\Quantun+Testing\OFFICIAL\quantum-testing"
D:\FPT\Study\2026\sem5\SWT301\Quantun+Testing\OFFICIAL\.venv\Scripts\python.exe -c "from quantum_testing.problems.risk_problem import RiskAwareProblem; p=RiskAwareProblem.from_matrix_csv('datasets/defects4j/Chart/1b/matrix.csv', risk_seed=12345, cr_threshold=0.95); print(p.n_tests, p.n_requirements, p.mutation.shape[1])"
```

Run tests:

```powershell
D:\FPT\Study\2026\sem5\SWT301\Quantun+Testing\OFFICIAL\.venv\Scripts\python.exe -m pytest -q tests/test_metrics_mo.py tests/test_risk_problem.py tests/test_ar_qiea.py tests/test_nsga2.py
```

Run full benchmark:

```powershell
D:\FPT\Study\2026\sem5\SWT301\Quantun+Testing\OFFICIAL\.venv\Scripts\python.exe scripts\pareto_benchmark.py --root datasets\defects4j\Chart\1b --seeds 42..71 --pop 40 --gens 150 --algorithms ar_qiea,mo_qiea,nsga2,random_front --risk-seed 12345 --cr-threshold 0.95 --risk-alpha 1.0 --archive-size 50 --output artifacts\pareto\chart1b_full_19-06-2026.json
```

Open/view outputs:

```powershell
Get-Item artifacts\pareto\chart1b_full_19-06-2026.json
Get-Content REPORT_EVERY_CHANGES\1B_Chart_Detail-Result-Analyst_19-06-2026.md
```
